# LAYER 4, ROUND 2: KOMMENTARE MINING — AVATAR LEVEL TAGGING

**Date:** 2026-05-24

---

## KEY FINDINGS & INSIGHTS

1. **Level 2 dominance confirmed**: Among autism-identified posts, Level 2 (19) is the largest segment, supporting the Layer 4 hypothesis that Level 2 is the most vocal autism segment.
2. **Level 3 underrepresentation continues**: Only 18 Level 3 posts despite ~25% expected audience share. This is a persistent data quality gap identified in Round 1.
3. **Group composition**: The Kommentare source is a general potty training Facebook group, not autism-specific. 2117/2180 (97%) of posts show no autism signal, representing the General Fallback audience.
4. **Pre-K urgency is the dominant Level 1 driver**: Almost all L1-coded posts mention school/preschool enrollment deadlines.
5. **'Tried everything' is pervasive even in General**: The phrase appears in non-autism posts too, confirming it's universal potty training frustration, not autism-specific.
